  492. A lot of skincare serums promise vitamin C but it's important to actually check the ingredients. There's no \\"best\\" type of topical vitamin C, but the most effective and stable is ascorbic acid, sodium ascorbyl phosphate and a few others. This serum has sodium ascorbyl phosphate which is encouraging. Most of the research has focused on 0.3% to 10% concentration ranges. This serum rings in at 20%. Is more necessarily better? There's no way to know, but it's great that they've packed more than the minimum studied amount rather than burying vitamin C somewhere deep in the ingredients like most other skincare products do.
